Why ETH wont go down after the Merge:  1. Big portion of staked ETH is from large validators who are in it for the yield not price gains.  2. ETH staking rewards should double to about 8% APY, which is very attractive. Migration from PoW to PoS will eliminate miners and therefore payments to miners will be replaced by smaller block rewards to staking validators.  3. Most invested at much higher ETH price levels, so are underwater and would be selling at a loss.  4. About 33% of staked ETH is through liquid staking platforms like Lido, which are already tradeble.

Why ETH not going down after the Merge: 1. Big portion of staked ETH is from large validators who are in it for the yield not price gains.  2. ETH staking rewards should double to about 8% APY, which is very attractive. Migration from PoW to PoS will eliminate miners and therefore payments to miners will be replaced by smaller block rewards to staking validators.  3. Most invested at much higher ETH price levels, so are underwater and would be selling at a loss.  4. About 33% of staked ETH is through liquid staking platforms like Lido, which are already tradeble.
